\DoxyCodeLine{77     \textcolor{comment}{// (https://tc39.es/ecma262/\#sec-\/canonicalnumericindexstring), where not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78     \textcolor{comment}{// finding such an index (either because of OOB, or because it's not a valid}}

\DoxyCodeLine{85     \textcolor{comment}{// Interceptors are API-\/level hooks for optionally handling a lookup in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86     \textcolor{comment}{// embedder code -\/-\/ if their handling returns false, then we should continue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87     \textcolor{comment}{// the iteration, though we should be conscious that an interceptor may have}}
